¶the cōfutacyon tyndale answere made syr thomas knyght lorde chaūcellour englonde ¶prentyd london wyllyam rastell 1532 cvm priv 〈…〉 ¶the preface crysten reader lorde sende v nowe yeres plentuouse good corne haue hadde yeres late plentuouse euyll bokes haue growen faste sprongen vppe thykke full pestylent errours pernyciouse resyes haue enfected kylled fere mo sely symple soules thē famyne dere yeres haue destroyed bodyes surely lytle cause drede great haboundaunce plentye tone lytle cause occasyon great derth scarcite tother syth lorde especyall prouydence vseth temporally punyshe hole people synnys parte cō pell good folke forbere abhorre noughty wherby maye brynge amendement auoyd selfe cōtagyō theyr cōpanye wysdome v perceyue y• lyke folke beginne delyte fedyng theyr soules venemouse caryn poysened heresyes whyche maye well veryfyed wordes holy wryt 4 regum 4 deth pot lorde lykewyse agaynwarde reuenge yt wythall begynneth wythdraw hys gracyouse hande frutes erth mynyshynge fertylyte corne catell bryngynge derth myche men remedy fully fynde cause yet bysyde thys somwhere sendeth warre sykenesse mortalyte punyshe fleshe odyouse hatefull synne soule spoyleth frute maner vertues meane vnbylyefe false fayth infydelyte tell one playne englyshe heresye say god nowe bygynneth fere surely excepte folke begynne reforme fawte ye soner god shall fayle suche wyse go forwarde shall well perceyue fele thencreace greyfe gere hytherto begynning yet prophete hely wryten thyrde boke kynges infydelyte idolatry vsed israell hartye prayour made vnto god kepte whole cuntre frō rayne space iii yeres halfe euyll wyll malyce deuocyon pytye payne pynchynge bodyes compell men remember theyre soules whyche ellys parell peryshynge false idolatrye nowe yt bolde shamelesse heretyques haue longe whyle neyther letted ceaced falsely insymulate accuse chyrche god callynge good crysten people idolatres honourynge sayntes reuerēt byhauour vsed theyr image yet haue done farre agaynste theyr owne conscyence whyche selfe well wote chirche vseth sayntes ymages none honour ordinate honouryng image sayntes sake sayntes ye sake god neyther image saynte saynt god knoweth say tyndale hym selfe well thereby farre hath rayled agaynste owne conscyence nowe laste answere boke retreateth farre bakke reuoketh almoste euer sayde byfore fayne graunte cristen men may haue image knele byfore ye shall hereafter se shall come place tother syde saye playnely vnto thynges wherwyth corrupte worlde infydelyte faythlesse idolatrye moste cursed kynde chyefe euyll idole yt yt bare name god eyther yt selfe deuyll yt represented beyng reputed wurshyped god robbed reuerence deuoute honour fro god tyndale calleth heresyes name fayth maketh men serue deuyll whyle wene serue god abomynable idolatrye yt idolatry put truste ye deuyll serue deuyll wyth fayth yt worse idolatrye make men wene serue god wyth fayth whyle dyspyte hym wyth false bylyefe yf infydelyte turkes byd men byleue machometes alchoran yt infydelyte tyndale hath done purposely mysse translate crystes holy gospell sette forth heresyes euyll alchorane yf idolatry ye paynēs dyd make idole god yt muste nedes myche worse idolatry heretykes call god cause euyll therby make god vayne idole deuyll worse kynd infydelyte • make bokes heresyes call ryght fayth abomynable infydelyte abuse scrypture god colour theyr false bylyef • worse bylyefe byleue sacramentes god hath ordeyned holy spyryte inuencyons man tyndale sayth confessyon inuencyon deuyll worse bylyefe byleue goddes word byleued yf yt put wrytyng worse bylyefe byleue y• mennis good wurkes neuer well done yet nothyng worthe man neuer better rewarde commyng towarde man heuen wurse bylyefe thē byleue man doth wronge pray hys father soule wurse bylyefe byleue man may sleyghtely regarde whytson sonday • hokke monday boldely eate fleshe good frydaye shroue tuysdaye wurse bylyefe byleue yt none synne dampne man onely lakke bylyefe yf yt idolatryes farre excede • passe incomparbly offende maieste lorde god secretynge vppe beel baal belzabub deuyls hell wherfore lyke place heresyes haue taken deper rote ben sprede abrode god hath taken depe sore vengeaunce onely derth deth also batayle sworde yt fered receypte pestylent bokes lorde sendeth v lakke corne catayle begynnynge wyll fayle yf faute mended sende v sore punishemēt hath sent redy suche place wolde lyke warnynge mended accordynge sayth xxvi chapyter leuiticus speketh wyse ye wyll geue eare vnto fulfyll commaundementes sette lawes naught despyce iudgementes leue thynges vndone ordeyned breake pacte couenaunt wyll agaynwarde thynges folowynge vnto wyll hastely vysyte wyth penury brennynge hete feuer whych shall sore vexe greue eye consume euen ye deth ouer thys ye shall sowe sede vayne ennemyes shall deuoure shall also set face agaynst ye shall fall byfore aduersaryes made subiectes vnto hate ye shall f • e man chaseth yf ye wyll yet thys obaye shall synnes adde put plage seuenfolde shall trede downe pryde stobernes forth doth properly fall daunger commynacyon threte dyspyse crystes sacramentes whyche hys holy ordynaunces great parte cristes new law testament shall lesse set hys commaundementes vppon boldenesse onely fayth set good workes nought lytell force daunger theyr euyll dedes vppon boldenesse bare fayth sleyght repentaunce wythout shryfte yeres luther hym selfe hys felowes afterwarde new sectes sprongen whych lyke ye chyldren vippara wold gnaw theyr mother bely ye bare name bokes almoste inough make boke euery sort bokes brought thys heresyes freshe whereof god hath iustyce synnys requytte tone mote mercy grace amende tother speke frere barn booke surely theyr bookes yet came abrode englysshe whych neuer one wyse good neuer none yet bad folysshe false hys hath synnes hys comynge ben playnely proued hys face wyse bokes cyteth alledgeth hys booke brought forth hym hys ignoraūce shewed hym hym selfe dyd dyuerse thynges confesse hys ouersyghte • clerely knowleged myssetaken wronge vnderstanden place suche wyse fynally confounded wyth shame mameryng whyther wolde retourne agayne ouer see tary styll renounce hys heresyes agayne tourne agayn crystes catholyke chyrche therfore desyred myghte haue lerned man present assygned vnto hym ferther instruccyon hys conscyence whyche hys request graūted hym wyll ferther come theron god knoweth god gyue hym ye grace amende euery good mā wyll glad therof haue farre gone agaynste goddes trewth therby greued god wyse god haue redy gyuen hym ouer euer ellys yt though god offer hys grace agayne malyce mannes wyll wythstande yet reiecte dowted god wyll fynde tyme hym well inough shew iustyce hym hath done vppon namely late swycherland vppon zuinglius fyrst brought barn heresye thyther concernyng sacrament aulter hense shall sure haue leue departe saufe accordynge kynges saufe conducte yet hath demeaned hym selfe synnys hys comynge hyther hath clerely broken forfayted hys saufe myscheuouse sortes bokes hadde yet kynges gracyouse forgyuenes yt proued bothe mennys owne confessyon occupyed aboute two thynges one wyt sewyng remyssyon perdon hys offence bryngynge bokes therwith euangelicall brethern england ellys causynge taken george constantyne ere escaped redy haue worde leste wyse abiured holy doctryne herte god know peraduēture deuyll yf entēded otherwyse surely entended toward hym somwhat good dealynge byfore deserued mych fauour mynded hym semed penytent mysse vsynge hym selfe fallynge tyndale heresyes agayne whyche knowleged hym selfe worthy hanged hadde falsely abused kynges graciouse remissyon pardon geuē hym byfore hadde whyle bought solde heretycall bokes secretely set forth heresyes wherof shewed hym selfe repentaunt vttered dysclosed dyuers hys companyōs abiured synnys wyste well abiured namely rycharde necton whyche constantynes deteccyon take commytted newgate except happe dye byfore pryson stādeth grete paryll ere longe hys fallynge agayne tindale heresyes burned thus semed maner george constantyne whyle pryson sore dyd forthynke hys errours heresyes perceyued pestylent poyson thoughte better infecte therwyth myghte meane hys deteccyon amended wyth losse hys body soule cured bothe twayne caste awaye yf man peraduenture hard herte malycyouse mynde incurable thought better sende hym deuyll alone let hym lyue drawe many wyth hym thys good mynde semeth constantyne therfore good hope hys amendemēt peraduenture man hadde amended standen styll grace yf euyll cōsayle • ad comen hym lefte vnsought deuelyshe inuencyon meane sende hym mych one letter fortuned intercepte selfe wryten vnto hym one iohn̄ byrte otherwyse callynge hym selfe adryane otherwyse iohn̄ bokebynder yet otherwyse tell trouth george constantyne hadde confessed vnto faythfull seruaunt myne declared necton deliuery many heretycall bokes sent worde forthwyth nec • sholde sende bokes home • whyche yf dyd myghte haue yet seen sure token amendement man constantyne perceyued well ben yet lykely haue fauour shewed hym necton one made byrte hys counsayle dyuysed bytwene necton sholde wyse affermynge constantyne coude done happely coude dede peraduenture solde redy necton syth taken sayed hys wyfe burned well knowen necton hym selfe man hys also solde many bokes heresye bothe london othey shyres syth abiuracyon euer mater byrte hys letter aduysed constantyne yf myghte possyble call bakke hys cō fessyon agayne wherin thynke good ye hys letter selfe lo wordes wrote grace peace sauyour iesus good brother cōstantyne syr ye mater ye wold haue brought passe maner wyse person home shold receyue stuffe delyuer accordynge vnto mynde therfore yf ye haue spoken farre mater maye none preiudyall hurte vnto wolde ye shold go ferther mater euyn man armed wyth fayth go forth mater boldely put theyr proues one none knowe well law god man thynge sende word ye shall fynde redy power euen dethe goddes grace praye longe preserue comforte trouble confusyon tyrauntes lo haue ye herde apostolycall pystle counsaylynge man go bakke wyth trouth arme hym selfe wyth fayth make hym stronge lye lowde forswere hym selfe yf nede byrt wyste well lykely leue byleue hym hys bare worde wyll byrt peraduenture preche brynge v mydwyues egypt saued chyldren israell pharao whych god gaue thē new howses wherin byrt wyll myche dyspute god hath gyuen hym howse • et one wyth lye saue yonge innocent babe wyth periurye defende olde pestylēt heretyke though saynt austayn sayth lawfull lye nothyng yet tell tale lay lye hyghly suche mennes charge folke whose hole secte nothyng el lye reherse letter bycause ye shold se trewth suche folkes wordes constantyne sayed semed pryson penytēt vtterly mynded forsake suche heresyes heretykes euer profe wherof onely detected sayd hys owne dedes felowes also studyed deuysed deuelysshe bokes whyche hym selfe hys felowes hadde brought shypped myghte come bys • hoppes handes burned therfore shewed shypmannes name markes ferdellys whych haue synnys hys escape receyued maye goddes grace though man fledde hense fere suche harme wyste hadde well deserued yet nothynge towarde hym peraduenture good ware yet amended hys mynde hath harte forsaken tyndale heresyes pray god wold sory euer tyndale sholde glory boste hys burnynge meane whyle tyll maye well appere surely turned catholyke fayth agayne wyll aduyse good crysten folke specyally kynges subiectes forbere estyew hys company ye englysshe man whyche shall foūden famylyare wyth hym byfore hys conuersyō knowen proued maye therby brynge hym selfe suspycyon heresye happely therof hys retournynge hyther also tyndale hyghly reioyceth burnyng tewkesbery se grete cause yf reken grete glory man dyd abyde styll stake faste bounden heresyes wolde haue abiured agayne wyth hys harte haue accursed tyndale yf ye myghte haue saued hys lyfe gaue counsayle vnto one iamys heresye pryson wyth hym iamys hath synnys confessed tewkesbery sayed vnto hym saue self abiure bycause haue abiured byfore remedy wyth buth deth whych wordes yf ben dyspayre lyfe well appereth wold wyth good wyll haue one abiured one periured agayne yet hys examynacyon denyed euer hadde holden opynyons abiured notwythstandyng hys axamynacyon person present myche honestye wourshyppe two ben present hys abiuracyon byfore whyche also hys owne hand subscrybed afterwarde beynge ferther examyned vppon ye denyed defended agayne amonge thynges sayed vsed praye sayntes byleued goddes frendes theyr prayours profytable v well done praye wheruppon sayd vnto hym selfe yt glad se hym poynte yet amended shewed hym trouth dede amys helde contrarye hadde greate truste tewkesbery dowted sholde tewkesbery hadde reuoked poynt wolde reuoke sone tewkesbery herd went agayne farre fynally wolde agre day dome eyther saynt heuen soule purgatory hell eyther ryght fayth sacrament aulter wolde confesse wyse thynges dyuers horryble heresy • delyuered laste vnto secular handes burned neuer wretche wene better worthy yet one thynge notable well declarynge good cherytable mynde mā dyed • delyuered vnto secular handes neyther whyle pryson tyme hys deth wolde wyll aknowen hys heresyes vnto man asked hym questyon couered hyd meanes coulde make labored make euery man wene yt neuer holden opynyon thys dealynge euery man maye se rought mych heresyes toke owne mynde suche thynges gretely forced whyther went forwarde bakwarde wolde fayne leue opynyon amonge people hys iudges borne hym wrong hande condempned hym heresyes neuer helde conscyence dyed mynde good man dowteth examynacyō secrete folke inough therat bothe spyrytuall temporall eyther parte ryght wourshypfull hys malycyouse mynde poynte lytell take effecte yet dyd iamys also confesse afterwarde tewkesbery redde vnto hym wyclyffes wykke • agaynst blessed sacrament ouer founden hym shyryffes offycers pryson boke heresye hys owne hande wrytynge wyt boke marten luther wherin teacheth men vnder name crysten lybertye rōne deuyls bo • dage hys howse founden tyndale boke obedyence whyche well alowed hys wykked boke also wykked mammona sayenge hys examynacyon heresyes therin good crysten fayth beynge dede full false heresyes frantike euer heretyke made syth cryst borne yet thys notwythstandynge shyryffes warde tyme hys deth wolde speke hys heresyes thynge say helde wolde holde thys poynt handeled hym selfe couertly coude make people wene hadde holden maner opynyon neuer thynke yf tyndale vngracyouse bokes neuer come hys hande whych pore wreche lyeth hell cryeth hym tyndale yf amēde tyme lyke fynde hym come togyther hote fyrebronde burnynge hys bakke water worlde wyll neuer able quenche another also hys vnhappy bokes haue brought vnto fyre tho bylney thas abiured whyche man wythout name spake mych dyaloge whyche beyng conuycte xx wytnesses aboue dyd yet stykke styll hys denyall sayd sorsworen vtterly belyed hym god whyche trouth bryngeth last alwaye trouth lyght wolde suffer suche obstynate vntrouth length passe vnpunyshed hys endles mercy brought hys body deth gaue hym yet ye grace turne saue hys soule dyuerse sermon whyche hys abiuracyon agaynst prohybycyon gyuen hym vppon hys abiuracyon made sundry secrete corner also openly wherof bysshoppe yet bycause herde none heresye therin forborne lay dysobedyence hys charge went vnto wych enfected dyuers cytye beynge secretely kepte certayne space whyle resorte vnto ancresse began secretely sow hys cocle brought vnto dyuers tyndale bokes taken doynge bokes founden nother man conuayenge thense thynges herde hole processe cam suche wyse passe coulde nothynge dowbte came lyght prouysyon god came examynacyon waxed styffe stoborne hys opynyons yet god good gracyous lorde vnto hym fynally fully conuerted vnto cryste hys trew catholyke fayth yt onely fyre well wordes wrytynge also many dayes reuoked abhorred detested suche heresyes holden whych notwythstandyng lakked sory sayd wrote norwych londō reuoked heresyes styll abyden suche ashamed thus saye wryte beynge afterwarde examyned theruppon saw cō trary playnely proued theyr face suche hys execucyon stode hym whyle redde hys reuocacyō hym selfe conclusyon nothynge elles say • redde hys reuocacyon softely coude confessed loked vppon byll redde sayd coude tell whyther byll hys reuocacyon yet rehersed selfe certayne thynges spoken hym ye peple fyre wherby coude perceyue well reuoked hys errours albe watered wordes wyth addycyons theyr owne well proued coude also deny forthwyth vppon hys iudgement hys degradacyon kneled downe bysshoppes chauncellour presence people humbly bysought hym absolucyon sentence excōmunycacyon wyth iudgement helde hym selfe well content knowleged yt well deserued suffer deth wyste sholde coude say nay vppon thys hys humble request prayour presence people assoyled byfore caryed court whyche selfe well wyste wolde neuer haue ben yf hadde reuoked yet nother thynge coude deny sayd therat yet hadde herd suche wyse sayd byleued trew thynge suche selfe alone muste nedes make sure reuoked hys heresyes thynge thys labored made greate instaunce certayne dayes hys iudgement myght suffred receyue blessed body cryste forme brede wherin chauncellour made whyle greate stykkynge dyffycultye entent wolde ye better clerely perceyue deuocyon man hadde fynally perceyuynge hym trew perfyte fayth hys desyre procede feruent mynde agreed graunted theruppon howseled trew perfyte fayth grete deuocyon euery good crysten man hath greate cause reioyce therin hys confessour ende masse bylney full deuowtely herde vppon hys knee brought vnto hym body cryste vppon paten y• chalyce wyth good godly exhortacyon vsed vnto hym excepte herte worde outwarde semblaunce shold ellys forbere receyue blessed body syth sholde vndowtedly receyue hys owne dānacyon wold haue gladded good crysten herte haue herd hys faythfull crysten answere reporte testyfye tyme moreouer presence holy sacrament holden yet vppon paten prestes handes bylney byfore receyued sayd y• colecte domine iesu christe came wordes ecclesiae tuae pacem concordiam dyuers tymes repeted wordes wyth tunsyons knok kynges vppon hys breste vnto god confessed asked mercy greuousely erred y• point sore offended hym co • tempnynge hys chyrche meruayle though specyall remorse artycle contempnyng crystes catholyke knowen chyrche framynge secrete vnknowen chyrche lerned luther tyndale ye poynt broughte hym vnto hys myschyefe fundacyon wheruppon heresyes byelded therfore ye goodnesse god gaue hym grace cast vnto deuyll hys errours gaue hym hys specyall grace haue heresye grounde remanaunt moste especyall repentaunce remorse wherby may well hope trust lorde whose hygh goodnesse gaue hym suche grace fully repente reuoke hys heresyes wyth glad herte content suffer fyre punysshement hys offence hath hys infynyte mercy taken accepted payne farre wyll exacte pore mannes purgatory settyng merytes hys owne paynefull passyon therunto hath forthwyth fyre taken hys blessed soule heuen prayeth incessauntly repentaunce amendement suche haue ben hys meanes whyle lyued suche errours induced confyrmed fermely truste goddys grace effecte wyth holy mannes prayour wyll worke praye god maye thus ye se ye tyndale hath greate cause glory hys martyr theyr lyuyng openly nought theyr opynyons suche hym selfe wyll abhorre redy abiure agayne yf myghte saue theyr lyfe theyr sectes dysperate eyther dare fyre set forth theyr opynyons shame ellys malyce dyssymule bryng ye people false opynyon theyr iudges wene iudged wronge bylney lernynge ben accustumed morall vertues god reuoked tyndals heresye ere dyed lykelyhed rather bycause god wolde haue good workes loste yet gloryeth tindale vngraciously theyr destruccyon r • kenynge theyr paynefull deth doth grete worshyppe hys bokes whyche suche sorte neuer worse abomynable wryten yet hys bokes beynge suche folke wyth suche folysshe fauour suche blynde affeccyon rede theyr taste enfected wyth feuer heresyes onely decerne thynge rede whyche yf coude good waye towarde amendement also dyscontent angry wyth man wolde helpe perceyue fayne wolde haue rather byleued answered whyche sorte haue asked haue medle wyth mater sayenge beynge laye man sholde leue clergye wryte hauynge professed study holy scrypture sholde leue mater hole vnto deuynes surely fyrst touchyng lernyng yf mater dowtfull thynges greate questyon hadde bene connyngly handeled tyndale hys felowes myghte seme therby mater greate dowte questyon wolde peraduenture lette alone selfe debated men erudycyon lernynge mater beynge playne euydent clere hole chyrche cryste clerely put questyon playne open heresye erenestly brynge questyon neuer purpose beynge ryght mynde trew crysten man gyue heretyque myche authoryte • eken selfe vnable playne poyntes crysten fayth answere hym namely syth haue gone somwhat scole selfe bestowed many yeres studye vnder connynge maysters haue se hytherto mater handeled suche wyse tyndale best bysyde euer haue wryten therin ryght meane lerned man almoste vnlerned woman hauynge naturall wyt beynge sure faste trewe catholyke fayth well able answere helpe god nothynge fynde effectuall amonge shamelesse boldenesse vnreasonable raylynge wyth scryptures wrested awrye made mynyster mater vnto theyr iestynge scoffynge outragyouse rybaldry onely agaynste euery estate erth agaynst moste moste relygyouse lyuynge also agaynste sayntes heuen agaynste blessed body cryste holy sacrament aulter whyche thynges fare folke truste nothynge elles wery wryters last wyth endlesse importune babelynge ouerwhelme hole worlde wyth wordes y• cause wrytynge mych debate dyspute thynges wyth whyche though truste therin gyue grete place many men maye mych better yet gyue men warnynge myschyefe theyr bookes bycause many good symple folke byleuynge men neyther saye meane euyll borne hande longyng therfore rede theyr bokes se thynge selfe fyrste infecte wyth heresyes seme fyrste intolerable ere euer come greatest beynge infecte wyth lesse fall laste bere greater whyche begynnynge coude neuer haue abyden yf wyll aske body gyue warnynge yes mete dede yet amonge parte apertayneth well knowe kynges hyghnes whyche hys moste faythfull mynde god thynge effectually desyreth mayntenaunce trewe catholyque fayth wherof hys honorable well deserued tytell defensor nothynge detesteth pestylent bokes tyndale suche sende realme sette forth theyr abomynable heresyes wythall doth hys blessed dysposycyon erthly thynges abhorre necessyte punysshement cause hath onely hys moste erudyte famouse bokes bothe englysshe latyn declared hys moste catholyque purpose entent also hys open proclamacyons dyuers tymes iterate renewed fynally hys owne moste roiall person sterre chamber moste eloquently hys owne mouth greate presence hys lordes spyrytuall temporall gaue monycyon warnynge iustyces peace euery quarter hys realme assembled byfore hys hyghnes theyr cuntrees hys people declared dyd prohybyte forbydde vppon greate payne bryngynge redynge kepynge pernycyouse poysened bookes entent euery subget hys meane suche manyfolde effectuall warnynge wyth hys gracyouse remyssyon theyr formar offence hys commaundement byfore broken sholde thense forthe auoyde estyew parell daunger punyshement dreue hys hyghnesse necessyte thynge whyche myldenesse hys benygne nature abhorreth seyng ye kynges gracyouse purpose thys poynt reken beynge hys vnworthy chauncellour appertayneth sayed vnto parte dewty folow ensample hys noble grace pore wyt lernynge wyth openynge hys people malyce poysō pernycyous bokes helpe mych yt hys people abandonynge contagyon suche pestylent wrytynge maye farre infeccyon therby suche punyshement folowynge theruppon doth aftentymes rather serue make beware yet clere cure hele well redy infected harde carbuncle catchynge onys core meane well surely cured god worketh somtyme towarde helpe wherof yf happely incurable clene cuttynge ye parte infeccyon remanaūt myne offyce vertue myne othe euery offycer iustyce thorow realme rate ryght especyally bounden reason onely good congrewence also playne ordynaūs statute wherfore recon selfe dewtye depely bownden shew good reders parell bokes wherof maker haue myscheuouse mynde boste glory theyr vngracyouse wrytyng bryngeth eny man deth yet make semblauns though sory yt tyndale cryeth owt vppon prelate vppon temporall prynces callethe theym murtherers martyr quellers dyssymulyng y• cruell wrech wyth hys wreched bookes murderethe man hym selfe whyle geueth hym poyson hys heresyes therby compellethe prynces occasyon theyr incurable contagyouse pestylence punyshe theym accordynge iustyce sore paynfull deth • bothe ensample infeccyon whych thyng sore heretyques reproue affermyng yt y agaynst gospell chryste eny heretyque persecuted punyshed specyallye bodylye payn dethe theym saye euery maner cryme thefte murder treason yet almayn contrary theyr owne euāgelycall doctryne euangelycalls theym selfe ceace pursew punyshe meany may purse pryson bodylye payne dethe dyuerse theyre euangelycall bretherne vary fro theyr secte coū terfayte euangelycalls mo sundry sortys dyabolycall sectes man may well reherse thys last dreuen theym selfe contrary theyre owne formar doctrine bycause fynde proue well experyence thoughe theyre sectes false heresyes yet tone sorte long dwell wyth tother yf begynne onys matchys shall fayle length contende stryue gether sedycyons tone dreue tother ruyne neuer shall y• cuntre long abyde wythout debate ruffle scysmes factyouse heresyes suffered whyle grow byleue yf eny man reken place euer founde otherwyse affryque ye donatystes grece ye arryanes boheme hussytes england wyclyffystes almayn lutheranes ye zuynglyanes bysynes haue made dystruccyon manslaughter haue caused partelye storyes wytnesse partelye men haue presentely seen yet hath god alwaye mayntened contynued hys trew catholyke fayth grete fall ruyne length many scysmatycall sectes whose fall vndowtedly remanaunt wyll conclusyon folow wyth playne open wrathe god shewed vppon theyr false prophetes fell vppon prophetes bothe beale baall thys yere vppon zuinglius hym selfe • fyrst brought swycherland abomynable heresye agaynst blessed sacrament awter say hande god thys yere slayne playne batayle agaynste catholikes many thousand wreched secte beyng nomber catholykes thre agaynst one prowdely wyth malycy • use purpose inuadynge euer dyd egypcyans pursew chyldren israell sayth tyndale frere barn bothe wronge call theyr bokes sedycyouse counsayle saye people theyr bokes obedyent vnto theyr souerayns ruler though shold suffer wronge bokes saye sedycyouse surely make men heretykes byd meke heresye spryngeth saynt austayne sayth pryde standeth well wyth reason make man dronke byd hym sober make hym starke madde byd hym well auysed make hym starke thefe byd hym se stele yt besyde ye sedicion euery scysine dyuisyon muste nedes moue prouoke amonge people yt dyuerse sectis though • edient vnto one prynce cause therby though rebelled agaynste person yet breke peace quiete cuntre tunne daynger parelle hys lawes let v yet ferther loke cōsyder maner fashyon counseyle people obay theyr prynces bydde people coūtenaunce obedient say therwyth lawys preceptes theyre souerayns nothynge bynde ye subiectes theyr conscyencys yf thynges cōmaundede forbeden cōmaunded forbeden scrypture y• wordes scripture wherby cōmaūded obay theyr gouernours wold restrayne vnto thynges onely expressede redy wythin corp scrypture yf begyle lawys preceptes theyr souerayns vnware men therby fle fro ye parell outwarde bodely ponyshemēt theyr euāgely call lybertie sholde serue theym suffycyently dyscharge theyre conscyence inwardely make theym theyre soules clere angelycall hypocrytys nowe whan falsely tell theym bounden obaye theyre gouernours lawfull commaundementes thenne holyly counseyle theym obay theyr vnlawfull tyranny name call lawys effecte wene ye wolde theyr aduyce sholde haue knowe theym selfe well ynough maner people madde warraūte yowe perceyue full well yf persuade people belyue yt theyr conscyence bounden obay ye lawes preceptys theyr gouernours theym selfe precyouse apostle folke wolde forbere theyre awne ease pleasure faynt fayned counseyle false apostatas thus y yt sure theyre false doctryne must yf belyued brynge ye people secrete contempte spyrytuall dysobedyence inwarde hatered lawe wherof muste folowe outwarde brech theruppon outwarde ponyshement parell rebellyon wherby pryncys sholde dreuen sore effusyō theyr subiectes blood hath redy mysse happened almayne olde tyme englande let v yet consyder ferther poynt theyr good holy counsayle concernynge people obedyence frere barn hys frantyke booke byddeth people sholde rebell wyse byddeth therwyth kynges cōmaundemēt shold suffer tyndale false translacyon scrypture go theyr hande rather dye leue knoweth well false malycyouse maner tyndale hath vsed translatyng therof • haue proued bothe dyaloge synnes agayne thys boke tyndale doth hym selfe hys owne answere openly confesse tytles penaunce preste done set forth hys false heresyes wythall therfore appereth well barn wold haue people rather dye obay theyr prynces puttynge away boke falsely translated mayntenaunce many pestylent heresyes thus ye se fayne wolde glorye people blode woteth well yt kynges hyghnesse wyll wyse wyse maye yf wyll saue hys owne soule suffer false translacyon handes vnlerned people whyche open heretyke purposely translated false destruccyon many soules man dowteth thynke tindale hym selfe wolde lesse done mayntenaunce hys false translacyon euangelystes wolde hys euangelycall brother barn folke sholde agaynste kynges proclamacyons kepe styll hys bokes rather leue dye quarell defence glory byfore dyaloge dyd say luther bokes sedycyouse say tyndale mouynge people theyr owne vndoyng dysobedyēt rebellyouse theyr souerayns affermyng bounden law made men tyndale answereth luther say vutrewly sayth ferther thys wyse crysten man bounden obay tyranny yf gaynste fayth law god tyll god delyuer hym therof let passe myche raylynge consequentely maketh vppon prynces shall thys tyme onely coū sayle consyder wordes hys whyche layeth forth rule people obedyence theyr prynce hys rule shall obay theyr tyranny tyll god delyuer therof thys poynt wyll tyndals interpretor may meane dyuerse wayes whych way meaneth dede shall hym selfe declare ferther • eysore thynketh meaneth well sauynge wyll take hym wurste tother poynt may bolde say good man may take hym well sayth crysten man y bounden obay theyre pryncys tyrāny yf agaynste hys fayth lawe god yet wyll well agre yt yf wordes spoken good faithfull mānys mouthe • nede requyred yt well sayed apostle sayed muste rather please god man tyndale y heretyke putteth rule people obedyence good crysten prynce bounden obay hys teranny yf yt agaynste fayth say rule obedyence y playne exhortacyon dysobedyence rebellion euery man well seeth yt tyndale amonge many abhominable heresyes techeth ye ryght faith freres may lawfully wedde nūnys man bounden ye kepynge fastyng day holyday made chyrch man sholde pray saynte pray crysten soules yt great synne wurshyppe crystys precyouse body blessed sacramente awter wolde people sholde kepe hys false translacyon scrypture mayntenance heresyes therfore yf prynce make lawe againste tyndale heresyes poyntes suche lyke tyndale teacheth tha • people boūden obay yt may must wythstande suche tyranny leste wyse though boūden peraduenture openly obaye theyr pryncis tyranny forberynge fleshe good fryday cōmynge goddes seruyce whytsone sonday freres forberynge open weddynge nōnes thinges yet tindale godly gospell theyr euangelycall lybertie secretely liste theym selfe peace brokē weke cōscience offended yet law cōmaūdemēt eyther prynce pope generall counsayle crysten nacyons angell wolde come heuen commaunde goddys name y• cōtrary euery mā must kepe still tyndale false translacyon scrypture abyde hys false bokes made mayntenaunce hys manyfolde false heresyes man muste law commaundement pray saynt soule purgatory kysse relyque crepe crystes crosse worshyppe crystes blessed body bloode holy sacrament aulter yf prynce wolde lawe commaundement compelle hys people thynges tyndale playnely teacheth maye muste styffely wythstande vnder god yet alwaye lernyd good men amonge hole people wyth necessarye artycles fayth confyrmed selfe see rome thynges amonge bygan disputable well appereth onely saynte chrysostome olde holy docto shall kepe promyse therfore say yt teacheth hys chyrch trewth meane trewth necessary hym self meant theyr saluacyon wytte suche thynge wyll vppon payne damnacyon haue bounden byleue say also vppon byleued nowe neyther necessarye byleue possyble thought vppon yt shall please god suche thynges shew reuele shall sende luther tyndale none huskyns frere nōnes bedde preache yt shall send suche holy sacramentes sette forth vyce boldenesse fayth prayse lechery betwene freres nōnes call yt matrymony thus make mokkes holy scrypture solemnely opē shamelesse abomynable blasphemy yf zele god amonge men shold raylyng rybaldes mokke wyth holy scrypture shold euery suche exposycyon haue hote iren thruste thorow theyr blasphemouse tonges false prophetes shall god saye sende none erand tyndale cā conscyence obedyence vnto preceptes lawes tradycyons men wryten scrypture thynge saynt austayne sayth dyuers holy men entreatyng wordes lyke allegorye doctryne preachynge saye confyrme • ykewyse neuer cōmaundemētes byddynges well appereth wordes folowynge byddeth shold obserue thynges saye sholde meane onely preceptes wryten law also theyr commaundementes besyde suche superstycyouse vnlawfull kepte clerely declared wordes cryste folowynge sayeth thys wyse bynde importable burdayns laye folkes shoulder self wyll put f • nger theyr owne therto though wolde saye syth syt vppō moyses chayre occupye hys place gouernours ye cōmaūde though burdayns bynde laye shoulder great heuy seme maner unportable wyll selfe leue vndone set onys fynger y• doyng warne know ryght well wordes maye well expowned tother fashyon afore remembred vnderstandyng allegory chayre moyses doctryne law moyses may greuouse importable burdayns called burden olde lawe wyth whyche saynt peter apostle contente wolde lade crysten people commynge vnto criste saynge neyther selfe theyr father coulde bere • em thus know well men may expowne wordes good men • holy men connynge men haue done lykewise maner twayne haue therein done well one texte maye dyuersely dyuerse sens expowned • though luther tyndale wyll haue one tyll nother may better make theyr owne purpose wyll let make fyftene though wordes may expowned yet sayde yt appereth well proper sense theyr owne tradycyons bysyde moyses lawe cryste sayde scrybes pharasyes dyd bynde greuouse burdayns importable lay mēnys shoulder euery man well woteth neyther scrybes pharysees dyd bynde lay mēnys shou • ders burden lawe lorde hym selfe whyche tyme whyle wolde yet haue thē kept wolde haue dyspraysed wyth callyng greuous importable though apostle dyd afterwarde tyme cam caste therfore haue sayde wordes crystes properly ment tradycyons commaundemētes scrybes pharasees selfe bysyde law whych thinges sauiour cōma • ̄ded kept obserued euer superstycyouse contraryed lawes commaundementes god tendynge honour vertue comen weale • place offyce scrybes pharysees kepte though selfe nought theyr good tradycyōs dyd neuer cryste dysprayse though somtyme dyspensed wyth dyscyples concernynge law man thynke madde • dowteth seruauntes mannys housholde bounden fulfyll obaye theyr maysters lyefull commaundementes yf wolde refuse hys byddynge knele downe say certayne praoyurs hym bed warde whole house gether tyll shold shew commaundement scrypture well worthy go deuyll theyr proude dysobedyence defence theyr false euangelycall fredome douteth saye thys whyche thynke good man douteth madde thynke neyther bysshoppe pope whole generall counsayle crysten people gether though assembled vppon playne able commaunde myche generall processyon vppon certayne daye lewde lyther losell lyste ryse may lye styll hys bedde say bounden obay mannys tradycyōs nothyng scrypture except auoydyng slaūder shalbe many ye processyon shall myssed yf man may say syke uppon wordes cōcernynge theyr tradycyons wold haue ben long sauyng frere barn rially triumpheth wyth agaynste lawes chyrch also tyndale answere xviii chapyter dyaloge bryngeth ye lyke entent entent properly proue bytwene ye may partely se yet farther shall goddes grace shall hereafter god wyllynge come touche place tyndale answere haue proued wordes crist make onely nothynge purpose agaynst ye lawes crystes chirche also make playnely lawes agaynste theyr purpose shall nede longe tary tother poynte wytte proue yt wordes cryste nothynge make agaynste pryncypall purpose nothynge proue yt euery necessary thynge wryten though constre crystes wordes tradycyons whyche properly spoken • de law moyses set therunto wordes saynte austayne also wyth whyche barn wolde seme well furnyshe mater fyrst crystes wordes yf hadde ben playne expressely euer scrybis pharysees bydde yt wryten law moyces warne se yt yet whyle sayde farther warne byleue thyng ellys wordes profe yt gether writen wher peple shold byleue thē yt thyng wher sholde byleue wryten moyses bokes whyche yf yt taken myghte teache people writen esaie • hieremie ezechiel cristes worde wyped oute credens therfore wordes expownynge doctryne moyses tradycyons scrybes pharysees yet nothynge proued byleued thynge sholde teache bysyde moyses bysyde ye scrypture neyther wordes cryste contrary myghte yet dayes trewthes kepte amonge people tradycyon begynnynge whyche scrybes pharysees bothe myght preache remember people myght scrypture therin byleued therfore sauyour sayd byleue thē nothing bokes moyses bokes scrypture sayd forbedīge thē byleue thē many thynges forbedyng folow theyr vyces cryste sayd farther iewes thynges necessarye wryten therfore byleue scrybes pharysees farther ye fynde wryten moyses prophetes thys proued thynge crystē • muste byleue wryten apostle euāgelistes • wordes saynt austayne whyche frere baron addeth therunto purpose nothyng auaunce mater saynte austayne applyeth wordes cryste preacher trew shepeherde kyng onely weale flokke ye pleasure criste mercennary hyred man preacheth luc •• wordely affeccyons hys owne sayeth yt chayre moyses vnderstande lernynge law god sayth therfore god dothe teache v wytte mercēnary preacher therfore teache law god thereafter wyll teache theyr owne doctrine yt yt suche men seke theyres crystes wyt theyr owne commodyte pleasure god lo sayth barn wordes saynte austayne playne agaynst preche thyng law god onely forthwyth well wyse • stede prechyng putteth ensample statute makyng though yt one thynge one man preche chirche make statute bycause ye shold se yet hys playnesse synceryte therin fayneth ye chirch maketh openly directly agaynst worde god destruccyon fayth statute sayth whereby haue condemned new testament also forbeden certayne men preache worde god hauynge cause agaynste onely theyr owne malycyouse suspycyon trouth statute made • thynge done neyther concernynge tone poynte tother new testament yf meane testament cryste yt condemned forboden neyther holy arche though euery man myght bolde touche yt trouth false englyshe translacyon newe testament newly forged tyndale altered chaunged mater great weyght malycyousely sette forth agaynste crystes trew doctryne tyndale antichrysten heresyes yt worthy called crystes testament eyther tyndale owne testament testament hys mayster antechryste therfore boke cōdemned well worthy condemnacyon therof neyther openly pryuyly directely indirectely agaynst ye worde god tendeth destruccion fayth cōsonaunt wyth worde god auferte masum ex vobismet ipsisand greatly tendyng mayntenaunce fayth concernynge testament haue dialoge secūde boke thys wurke well proued poynte wherunto tyndale weneth fynde farther defence let hym lay yt forth also statute made ye chirch forbyd man preache worde god hauyng cause agaynst hym theyr owne malycyouse suspycyon god dowte wyll neuer suffer hys chyrche fall madde make suche law frere barn fynde law made suche mater • let hym reherse waraunt shall fynde suche wordes dede law made bothe chyrche thys realme parlyament man shall suffred preache dyocyse agaynste bysshoppes wyll wene law agaynst goddes law agaynste reason neyther excepte eyther goddys lawe good reason sholde suffer one man sholde medle wyth another mannes charge magry teeth ye charge bylongeth ellys shold suffred sow shrewd seed heresyes scysmes sedycyōs among people fyrst • burned vp leysour folke suppose better prohybyted bytymes ere suffred longe go forwarde ye parell mennes soules theyr owne haue prohybited late whyche one yet sore set vppon euyll prechyng yt prohybycyon abiuracyō yet wold preche heresyes styll vntyll last god caused hym taken tindal bokes hym two burned togyder wyth profyte vnto soule thē ben happely haue lyued lenger dyed bedde mynde sholde haue dyed lorde knoweth know well dyed good crysten man wyste well reuocacyon coude saue body yet reuoked heresyes abhorred tyndals bokes saue hys soule serue well wordes saynte austayne agaynst barn whyche wordes barn bryngeth hym mercēnary precher heretykes tyme yt yf say aught well accordynge catholyke fayth shame saye nought one take preache theyr owne heresyes rewarde worldely prayse delyte theyr owne syngulare pryde seke theyr owne crystes putte sylence prohybyte preache thys allegorye wyll agre wyth ye sayd wordes saynt austayne crystes wordes yet mych ye better heretyques maye properly called onely mercennaryes saynt austayne speketh also scrybes pharisee wurse kynde criste gospel speketh false scribe wytte wryters wrytyng trew bokes scrypture false gloses contrary commentes vppon scrypture erronyouse bokes dyuelyshe heresyes dyuysed theyre owne frantyque braynes coloure wherof abuse scrypture lyste also denye ye scrypture also ye worst kynde pharysees haue dyuyded selfe people professyon honest vertuous lyuynge haue dyuyded selfe catholyque chirche cryste abomynable heresyes honeste people cōtempte good wurkes bestely professyon freres nonnes lyuyng gether lechery preachyng theyr horedome fo • honeste matrymony thynges whyche sholde vouchsaufe scrybes • e false pharysees preache deuyls deuyces theyr owne yt preached consonaunte catholyque fayth y goddes law whyther yt wrytē saynt austayn sayth preachynge onely scripture goddes law sayth wherein comphended euer boūden byleue wherof saynt austayn doth hym selfe confesse dyuerse thynges vnwryten ensample perpetuall virgynyte blessed ladye whyche byleueth bycause yt wryten saynt austayne calleth fals • heretyque hys boke wryten vnto quod vult deus doth saynte hierome hys boke agaynste eluidius thynges therfore partes plantes whyche father heuen planteth hym selfe hys apostle holy spiryte owne sonne abydynge hys chirche whyther wryten thus ye se good reders neyther wordes cryste saynt austayne neyther proue apostle haue lefte necessarye thynges wrytynge therfore though barn fonde brynge text purpose yet tyndale perceyued well yt wold serue therfore lefte yt yet layeth frere barn nother texte thys purpose ye wordes saynt poule wryten vnto timothe iii chapyter ye ii pystle saynte poule wryteth vnto hym thys wyse abyde thou thynges yt thou hast lerned yt betaken ye knowynge whō thou haste lerned thyn infancye thou haste knowen holy scrypture whyche maye instructe helth fayth yt cryste iesu scrypture inspyred god profytable teche reproue correcte teache men iustyce man god maye perfayte instructed euery good worke haue rehersed saynt poules wordes full thē doth frere barn bycause ye maye haue gesse lefte remanaūt reherseth ye chyrche muste neyther make law statute nothynge onely preache mynyster worde god nothynge addynge mynysshynge poule sayth timothe abyde thynges haue lerned commytted vnto se ye well saynte poule speketh nothynge timothe agaynst addynge • good order statute hys chyrche byddeth hym abyde faste thynges hath lerned hym hath lerned scrypture ioynynge scrypture alwaye ryght fayth cryste whyche lerned saynt poule therfore agaynste makynge law thys texte serueth frere baron strawe moreouer consydered saynte poule sayth timothe abyde thynges haue wryten abyde thynges thou hast lerned eyther scrypture ellys otherwyse • e wythout scrypture wrote vnto thessalonycēses obserue ye preceptes whyche haue gyuen eyther worde wrytynge wryteth vnto timothe pystle haue thou forme fasshyon holesome wordes whyche thou haste herde fayth loue cryste iesu sayth wordes haue wryten vnto ye thou hast redde myne wordes thou hast herd yet thys purpose texte saynte poule barn bryngeth forth another thynge cō sydered saynt poule telleth timothe haue ben lerned scrypture hys chyldhed yet must ioyne therwyth ye artycles fayth cryst may well appere gyueth timothe thys warnynge arme hym wyth agaynst heretyques whyche wolde labour colour apparent scryptures destroye fayth timothe lerned heretykes saye therfore noted yt saynt poule gaue timothe warnynge • sholde stande faste thynges hadde taught hym remembrynge lerned trew apostle • wolde tell hym contrary false heretykes must agaynste heretykes wolde draw v trew fayth haue lerned stande fast remember haue lerned • cryste hys apostle contynually hys perpetuall apostle catholyke chyrche cryste anymated instructed accordynge hys promyse wyth hys owne spyryte xvc yeres suche thes • bable agaynst false heretykes whose snakysshe serpentyne generacyōs haue euer hytherto haue crept adder snake somer theyr heddys trodē downe god good men saynt poule tolde timothe scrypture good profytable teache faythfull folke reproue heretykes yf ioyned therwyth alwaye fayth cryste wythout whyche wolde hym seruyce ben lerned therin hys chyldhed y• warnynge gyuen timothe saynt poule hath taught v also yf haue sure herte artycles crystes fayth whyche surely kepte cryste hys catholyque chyrche shall able well vnderstande scrypture mych shall suffyce necessary yf haue bylefe shall haue ryght vnderstādyng ryght byleyfe therby vnderstandynge scrypture though thynges wrytē therin wyll yet profytable stand v good stede onely instruccyon towarde perfeccyon vertuose lyuynge also dysputacyon agaynste heretykes bothe profe many artycles ryght bylyefe proue clerely comen consent crystes catholyke chyrche crystes trew fayth erre dampnably deceyued whyther thynges byleued wryten scrypture also hys catholyke chyrche y comen knowen chyrche crysten nacyons saue false heresyes separated fro vn tother syde wythout catholyque fayth cristes chirch fastened harte scrypture yt coulde haue serued timothe wythout trew fayth hadde harte yt serue v neyther confusyon heretykes spirituall profyte selfe thus ye se frere baron hath pore helpe texte saynt poule whyche thynge tyndale well percyued therfore lefte yt barn hym self perceyuynge moste parte wolde make mych agaynst hym toke lytle lefte remanaunt yet bryngeth barn nother texte saynte poule wryteth vnto romayns xv chapyter dare speke thynge god hath wroughte whyche wordes fyrste hard stande place old interpretours stode great doute saynte poule ment farre forth exposycyon saynte ambrose saynte poule ment nothynge perteyned glory prechyng worde god god fulfylled yt hym though wold say taught god taught gentyles hym origene expowneth nother maner saynt poule wordes ment wolde take vnto hym self prayse mennes dedys wolde onely speke suche thynges god wrought hym selfe theophylactus aloweth origenes exposycyon yet addeth thyrde therto sayenge person saynt poule boste yo • thynges haue done onely shew thynge haue done selfe yt haue done yt haue done yt cryste hath done yt shew good reders bycause ye shold somwhat perceyue maner men whyche vse many thynges proue theyr mater textes moste dyffycultye suche leste vnderstanden therfore mater lyberty mannys wyll predestynacyon ye mater fayth good wurkes passe ouer playne textes euangelystes wyth slayght glose theyr owne diuyse profe theyr owne parte rūne hard place gospell saynte iohn̄ apocalyps ye pystles saynt poule suche place almoste hard apocalyps whych expowne yt please call playne say euery man woman may vnderstand easyly notwythstandyng saynte peter beynge longe scole wyth cryste chyefe hys apostle protesteth openly worlde wrytynge saynte poules pystles haue thynges hard dyffycyle sayth farther suche barn tyndale • heretyque theyr felowes hard thynges sayth saynt peter wryten saynt poule men vnlerned vnstable depraue mysconstre remanaunt scrypture vnto theyr owne perdycyon saynt poule sayth hym selfe also • mater good wurkes false heretykes mysse cōstre hym sayeth therfore theyre dampnacyon y iuste ryghtuouse thus say heretyques laye forth theyre parte hard textes doutefull barn doth texte place yt standeth beste lerned men dowte constre yt yt let barn constre yt whych way lyste may haue hold wordes shall neuer serue purpose neyther concernyng forbedynge lawes made chirche proue euery thynge necessary saluacyon writen scrypture rather playne contrarye euery man well woteth euery necessarye thynge wryten saynt poule hath wryten euery thynge taught euery thynge dyd write therfore text saynt poule brought barn nothynge helpeth purpose rather greatly hyndreth yt whych thynge tyndale well perceyued therfore lefte yt oute tyndale saw well also thynge mayster marten luther layde lashed oute agaynste kynges hyghnes concernynge purpose spekynge agaynste tradycyons men serue purpose mater agaynste sacramentes poynte catholyque fayth whyche saye tradycyons god wherof tyndale well knoweth nothynge luther layed thynge proue contrary thynge touche purpose proue necessarye poyntes crysten fayth crystes apostle putte wrytyng therfore tyndale seynge mayster martine luther poynt rosseus shamfully sowsed myre byfore thought wolde beware pudle come nere yt therfore lefte yt mayster brought mater ther yet one texte remayned wherof many wonte bere theym hygh saynge saynt poule text tindale hath also brought forth ere thys proue muste byleue nothynge onely scrypture wryteth galathyes furst chapyter yf angell heuen wold come downe preache gospell hym selfe done accursed thys texte hath nowe frere barn brought freshe purpose hys new frantyke boke magnyfyeth mych hym selfe wyth tyndale hath left shame tyndale last longe lokyng espyed well yt yt wold nothyng serue hys mater saw well saynt poule ment none angell byleued yf taught contrarye gospell ment none angell byleued yf god sent hym conferme also shew somwhat god wolde haue done farther tyndale saw also texte sayeth saynte poule hath wryten hys owne gospell hys felowes hadde wryten yt amonge whyche wyste well poynte muste proued therfore frere barn folyshely bryngeth yt doth tyndale wysely leue yt surely haue sayde hys wytte serued hym well leuynge th • se hys wyt fayled hym one thynge hadde lefte oute also euer hath hym selfe brought whyche selfe se well haue nowe proued hym lytle preue hys purpose hym selfe seeth well tother dyd whyche cause ashamed speke haue ye herd farre fynde euer tyndale eyther hath sayde say mater eyther hym selfe man ellys profe hys owne parte dysprofe therby se ye well neyther hath proued neuer shall proue whyle lyueth neyther hym selfe man ellys thyng boldely sayth thynge necessary saluacyon wrytē scrypture able man ellys neuer shall hereafter able auoyde yt god taughte y yet bounden may teche wyll wyll wyth scrypture wythout may cō maunde yt byleued beyng contrary hath taught redy maye commaunde thynges done though contrarye thynges hadde hym selfe scrypture commaunded afore thynke yt dowted notwythstādynge moyses receyued law ad ceremony writyng yet receyued tyndale sayth dyd thyng fully wrytynge remayned people myndes bysyde wrytyng dyuerse thynges necessary great wayght hadde receyued byfore • kepte peraduenture adam owne dayes concernynge commynge cryste redempcyon hym state soules heuen hell purgatory paradyse lymbus patrum yt wyll lyste loke therfore well perceyued wrote moyses dayes iewes myche open lyght knowlege thynges bysyde appereth writē v bokis moyses whereby yt wyll well appere tyndale sayeth trew sayth moyses dyd put wrytynge ye shall well fynde also yt wythstādyng euer hath ben wryten synnys eyther prophetes euangelystes apostle yet wyll yt neuer appere wryten taught mouth y• chirche cryste hath taught vnto spiryte god dyuerse treuthes whyche good man doute wherof scrypture nothynge determyneth whyche thynges therfore false heretyques brynge questyon lette say contrary comen knowen ensamples ladyes perpetuall virgynyte assumpcyon blessed body whyche god wold ellys haue founden erth honored well bodyes saynt hym selfe hath caused specyall reuelacyon dyuerse sought founden • wurshypped erth hys sake confermed yt many manifest miracle fynde autentyque storyes tradycyons haue also ye prayeng saynts knowledge pray v yt ye boke machabe •• yet thynge well appereth tradicions haue holy lenton faste brotheles boldely take vppon breke lollardes eate fleshe whyche holy faste folys theyr wrytynge call folyshe faste haue also saterdaye chaūged ye sondaye whyche care turne frydaye haue halowyng chalyces vestymēts pascall taper holy water wyth dyuerse thynges tradycyons holy spiryte hath chirch also knowlege consecrate say masse thynge pray desyre therein thys haue also knowlege reuerēce image holy sayntes oure sauyour crepe hys crosse dyuyne honour vnto blessed sacrament auter whyche yet saye trouth neuer tradycyon neded syth scrypture y playne yt crystes owne precy • use bodye whyche y dede quykke wyth blessed • le wyth godhed vnseparably ioyned frantyque fole coulde doute yt sholde wyth dyuyne honour wurshypped though neyther god man bysyde knowledge hadde geuen v warnynge therof yet tyndale farre bysyde hym selfe byleueth scrypture god word spoken goddes owne mouth sayde yt hys owne body blasphemouse agaynst god calleth great synne blessed bodye cryste sacrament honour bycause yt y commaunded sayth scrypture thus may ye good crysten reader se poynt laste thys heresye bryngeth folke fyrste fall poynt regarde goddes word yf geue yt wrytynge • wythin whyle fall downe farre yt neyther regarde hys worde wrytynge yet hym selfe neyther nowe yt worlde se shyfte folke fayne seke sometyme come forth shamlesse boldely tell theyre tale yet perceyue myddes thereof theym wonder caste theyr hodes keuer theyr face shame somtyme say care scrypture alone set nought euer wrote synnys apostle dayes se agayn abyde word shamelesse restrayne vnto viii hundred yeres laste paste whyche saye corrupted graūte good men taught trewth saye wyll byleue though selfe wolde aske whyche olde men viiic yere last past euer sayed relygyous men myght runne wedde nonnes say nothynge fare though herd lorde rochester selfe mater yt haue hande proue dyuers thynges whyche chyrch vseth byleueth whych neuer made law wryten yet obserued thorow y• catholyke chyrche suche antyquyte euery man myghte well perceyue came y• apostle selfe h • layed forth greate clerke olde auncyent father origene wherwyth haue shewed tyndale angry rated origen called hym starke heretyke yet shall tyndale fere wythall thentent shall blynde make wene olde father thys mater hys mynde ye shall well se thynges whyche reproueth wolde haue wene nought worth bycause sayth scrypture thynges deuysed tyndale sayth popys popysh wythin thys viiic yere shall promysed byfore y• second boke reherse bothe wordes origene besyde vndowted holy mē synnes shall reherse dyuers viiic yere aboue xic yere aboue thousande lorde rochester hath gathered dyuerse togyther rehersed mater hys boke agaynst luther whyche saue origene onely tyndale dyssembleth bycause may call • tyke called origene haue poynt answered tyndale sayd seconde boke origene fyfte homely vppon boke numeri wryteth thys wyse obseruaunces chyrche thynges whyche muste necessyte obserued kept ye • cause appereth euery man ensample knele pray partes heuen moste specyally tourne v towarde este suppose man lyghtely knoweth y• cause moreouer sacrament thaulter eyther maner receyuyng guyse fashyon cōsecracyon formale wordes ceremonyes vsed baptysme questyons answeres vsed may well open declare reason yet thynges though coueryd hyd bere vppon shoulder tyme wyse accōplysh fulfyll haue receyued great byshoppe cryste hys chyldren delyuered commended vnto v damascene fourth boke xiii chapyter y• prayeng towarde oryente wryteth thus tradicyon apostle wryten many thynges delyuered vnto v wythout wrytynge farther xvii chapyter wryten y• • urshyppynge ymages sayntes sayeth many thynges holy apostle haue delyuered vnto v wythout wrytynge saynt poule apostle gentyles wryteth wyse stande faste obserue tradycyons whyche ye taught yt worde wrytynge vnto corynthyes thus commende ye brethern cause euery thyng ye haue remembred kepte tradycyons delyuered ye dyonise fyrste chapyter ecclesiasticae hierarchiae leders maysters crysten fayth sayth delyuered v many thynges kepte partely wrytynge partely theyr instytucyons vnwryten saynte cypriane sermon wasshynge fete hygh preste hym selfe ordayner author owne sacrament resydew men taught
